# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Define the Sine rule




















What are its use cases?
Finding the side length or angle in a triangle when you have a matching side and angle
Side and opposite angle pair is needed

When can it not be used.
When there is no pair of a side and an angle.

Question 2:
 ^TGWuV2ap

One assumption that we made is that the building is perpendicular to the ground / the ground is flat ^kgUaKyMJ

An assumption that we had to make is that it is an isosceles triangle, (the cable is staying the same length) ^BG82IlaY
